# CLAUDE.md

This file provides guidance to Claude Code (claude.ai/code) when working with code in this repository.

## What This Directory Is

`/home/t0n34781/brand/` is the **BADGR Technologies brand operating system** вЂ” the single source of truth for all brand identity, tone enforcement, content generation, and marketing output for BADGR Technologies LLC (Atlanta B2B SaaS).

This is not just a style guide. It is a structured RAG-ready system that any AI agent, pipeline, or Claude Code session can load and execute against.

---

---

## How to Load the Tone System (RAG)

**Entry point:** `tone-system/registry/badgr_registry.json`

**Minimum load for any content task:**
```
1. tone-system/enforcement/badgr_enforcement_policy.json  (always)
2. tone-system/core/badgr_core_tone.json                  (always)
3. tone-system/registry/badgr_intent_router.json          (route to correct module)
4. [matched module]
```

**Full load matrix:** see `tone-system/runtime/badgr_rag_instructions.md`

**Intent routing:** `tone-system/registry/badgr_intent_router.json` maps keywords like `"cold email"`, `"ad copy"`, `"tiktok"`, `"enforcement rule"` to their module files.

---

## Content System Commands

**To run the daily content pipeline**, load `content-system/master_prompt.md` as system context and follow the steps in `content-system/pipeline_spec.json`.

**Output destination:** `social/output/YYYY-MM-DD/daily_pack.json`

**Platform constraints:** `content-system/platform_rules.json` вЂ” character limits, posting windows, optimization priority per platform.

---

## Enforcement Rules (Never Override Without Explicit Flag)

- No fabricated statistics вЂ” write "results vary" if no verified data
- No competitor naming
- No banned phrases (see `tone-system/core/badgr_voice_rules.json`)
- Pricing must match `identity/pricing_tiers.md`
- AI-generated TikTok content в†’ label "Made with AI"
- Hashtags: 3вЂ“5 per post, always `#BADGRTech` + `#CTRLALTDELIVER`

---

## Integration With Other BADGR Systems

| System | Integration Point |
|---|---|
| `SocMed_Labs/` | Ingest `tone-system/` into ChromaDB via `social_lab_ingest.py` |
| `tiny_agent/` | Add tone enforcement as pre/post step on content skills in `skill_registry.json` |
| `n8n_Lead-Gen-Go/` | Load `registry.json` at pipeline start; route by intent node |
| Direct Claude Code | Load `tone-system/runtime/badgr_rag_instructions.md` as session context |

---

## Key Design Rules

1. **Tone is a constraint, not a style** вЂ” enforcement runs last, on every output.
2. **Load minimum viable modules** вЂ” don't inject the full system into every prompt.
3. **Enforcement over creativity** вЂ” if fail conditions are hit, regenerate; never patch.
4. **Platform character limits include spaces** вЂ” count accordingly.
5. **Original spec .txt files are preserved in `specs/`** вЂ” do not modify; they are the source record.
